    SELECT p."ProductId", p."AddedByVendorUserId", p."CreatedAt", p."Description", p."MainProductSubCategoryAttributeId", p."ProductApprovalStatusId", p."ProductName", p."ProductStatusId", p."ProductSubCategoryId", p."UpdatedAt", p."VendorId"
    FROM "Product" AS p
    WHERE p."VendorId" = @vendorid
    ORDER BY p."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @p2 OFFSET @p
) AS p1
INNER JOIN "ProductApprovalStatus" AS p0 ON p1."ProductApprovalStatusId" = p0."ProductApprovalStatusId"
INNER JOIN "ProductStatus" AS p2 ON p1."ProductStatusId" = p2."ProductStatusId"
INNER JOIN "ProductSubCategory" AS p3 ON p1."ProductSubCategoryId" = p3."ProductSubCategoryId"
INNER JOIN "ProductCategory" AS p4 ON p3."ProductCategoryId" = p4."ProductCategoryId"

    FROM "ProductVariant" AS p7

    ) AS s ON p7."ProductVariantId" = s."ProductVariantId"

) AS s0 ON p1."ProductId" = s0."ProductId"

FROM "CartItems" AS c
INNER JOIN "Cart" AS c0 ON c."CartId" = c0."CartId"
INNER JOIN "ProductVariant" AS p ON c."ProductVariantId" = p."ProductVariantId"
INNER JOIN "Product" AS p0 ON p."ProductId" = p0."ProductId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i."InventoryId", i."AddressId", i."AvailableQuantity", i."IsActive", i."ProductVariantId", i."ReservedQuantity", i."UpdatedAt", a."AddressId" AS "AddressId0", a."AddressLine", a."City", a."ContactName", a."ContactPhoneNumber", a."Country", a."CreatedAt", a."IsActive" AS "IsActive0", a."IsDefault", a."LandMark", a."PinCode", a."State", a."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0", a."UserId"
    FROM "Inventory" AS i
    INNER JOIN "Address" AS a ON i."AddressId" = a."AddressId"
) AS s ON p."ProductVariantId" = s."ProductVariantId"
WHERE c0."UserId" = @userId
ORDER BY c."CartItemsId", c0."CartId", p."ProductVariantId", p0."ProductId", s."InventoryId"
